## Text Curency for interface:


money_value_undervalued = {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no

	text = {
		trigger = {
			money_value_target_real > money_value_predicted_devaluation
		}

		localization_key = undervalued
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			money_value_target_real < money_value_predicted_revaluation
		}

		localization_key = overrated
	}
}
money_value_overrated = {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no

	text = {
		trigger = {
			money_value_target_real < money_value_predicted_revaluation
		}

		localization_key = overrated
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			money_value_target_real > money_value_predicted_revaluation
		}

		localization_key = undervalued
	}
}







subject_type_icon = {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no

	text = {
		trigger = {
			is_subject_type = subject_type_customs_union
		}

		localization_key = customs_union_texture
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
            is_subject_type = subject_type_protectorate
		}

		localization_key = protectorate_texture	
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			is_subject_type = subject_type_dominion
		}

		localization_key = dominion_texture
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			is_subject_type = subject_type_puppet
		}

		localization_key = puppet_texture
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			is_subject_type = subject_type_vassal
		}

		localization_key = vassal_texture
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			is_subject_type = subject_type_tributary
		}

		localization_key = tributary_texture
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			is_subject_type = subject_type_personal_union
		}

		localization_key = personal_union_texture
	}
}
